<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Project 16 - Yola's Portfolio</title>
    <link rel="icon" href="favicon.png" type="image/x-icon">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/styles.css">
</head>
<body>
    <header>
        <a href="index.html" class="header-link">
            <h1>Yola Vermehr</h1>
        </a>
        <h2>Crossing the Line</h2>
        <p>My grad project in college. <br>
            I was very interested in the unique skill-set that oil painters had in the 16 and 17 hundreds.<br>
            I used my fingers to create intricate lines celebrating the colors and details of these paintings. <br>
            Often creating a halo like effect around the women in these images.</p>
    </header>
    <main>
        <section class="gallery">
            <img src="media/project_16_media/p16-1.jpeg" alt="Image 1">
            <img src="media/project_16_media/p16-2.jpeg" alt="Image 2">
            <img src="media/project_16_media/p16-3.jpeg" alt="Image 3">
            <img src="media/project_16_media/p16-4.jpeg" alt="Image 4">
            <img src="media/project_16_media/p16-5.jpeg" alt="Image 5">
            <img src="media/project_16_media/p16-6.jpeg" alt="Image 6">
            <img src="media/project_16_media/p16-7.jpeg" alt="Image 7">
        </section>
    </main> 
</body>
</html>
